1115<div class="Primary_contentWrapper__evl1f" style="background:var(--yellow);color:currentColor">

Ensure that text and background colors have enough contrast.
The text color to background color contrast ratio after composition is: 2.02 with color: rgb(255,255,255)background: rgb(254,162,25)font-size: 16.00ptfont-weight: 500

Some users find it hard to read light gray text on a white background, dark gray text on a black background and white text on a red background.

  • The contrast ratio should be 3.0 or more for 18 point text, or larger
  • The contrast ratio should be 3.0 or more for 14 point bold text, or larger
  • The contrast ratio should be 4.5 or more for all other text

1152<h4 class="h4">

1153<br/>

1154A national dining event celebrating your local restaurant community.</h4>

1155<p class="p">

1156</p>

1157<p class="p light">

1158The James Beard Foundation’s Taste America® presented by Capital One brings together chefs, special guests, and diners from across the country to celebrate the local independent restaurants at the heart of our communities.<br/>

1159<br/>

1160The walk-around tasting at the Four Seasons Hotel San Francisco will be an exciting gathering of the San Francisco Bay Area culinary community, with food stations hosted by TasteTwenty chef <strong class="strong">

1161Nelson German</strong>

1162 of <strong class="strong">

1163alaMar Dominican Kitchen</strong>

1164 and <strong class="strong">

1165Sobre Mesa Afro-Latin Cocktail Lounge</strong>

1166 and many other notable local chefs. Each station will reflect the chef’s signature culinary style and highlight the uniqueness of their restaurant and community. The tasting will also have beverage stations and other activations from our national and local sponsors.</p>

This button element is empty and has no accessible name.

A programmatically determined name allows screen readers to tell users what the control does. To add a name do one of the following:

  • Add text between the button start and end tags
  • Add a title attribute
  • Add an aria-label attribute
  • Add an aria-labelledby attribute
  • Add an img alt attribute if the button contains an img element
img elements with role=presentation or role=none are not included in the button's accessible name.

The CSS outline or border style on this element makes it difficult or impossible to see the link focus outline.
:focus and :not(:focus) have same outline:
Do not remove the default outline style, and change any border styles to avoid obscuring the focus outline around focusable elements. See :focus-visible for more information.

Using a border or outline style that obscures the focus ring causes problems for keyboard-only users in:

  • Chrome (obscures the focus indicator on links, buttons, dropdowns and range controls)
  • Firefox (obscures the focus indicator on links)

Line 1820 WCAG 2.2 A 4.1.2 Section 508 (2017) A 4.1.2
This button element is empty and has no accessible name.

A programmatically determined name allows screen readers to tell users what the control does. To add a name do one of the following:

  • Add text between the button start and end tags
  • Add a title attribute
  • Add an aria-label attribute
  • Add an aria-labelledby attribute
  • Add an img alt attribute if the button contains an img element
img elements with role=presentation or role=none are not included in the button's accessible name.

1838The Grove Restaurant Logo</span>

1839</button>

The aria-labelledby attribute references a blank element.
Make sure aria-labelledby references an element containing text.
Line 1840 WCAG 2.2 A 4.1.2 Section 508 (2017) A 4.1.2
This button element is empty and has no accessible name.

A programmatically determined name allows screen readers to tell users what the control does. To add a name do one of the following:

  • Add text between the button start and end tags
  • Add a title attribute
  • Add an aria-label attribute
  • Add an aria-labelledby attribute
  • Add an img alt attribute if the button contains an img element
img elements with role=presentation or role=none are not included in the button's accessible name.
Line 1840 WCAG 2.2 A 4.1.2 Section 508 (2017) A 4.1.2
The CSS outline or border style on this element makes it difficult or impossible to see the link focus outline.
:focus and :not(:focus) have same outline:
Do not remove the default outline style, and change any border styles to avoid obscuring the focus outline around focusable elements. See :focus-visible for more information.

Using a border or outline style that obscures the focus ring causes problems for keyboard-only users in:

  • Chrome (obscures the focus indicator on links, buttons, dropdowns and range controls)
  • Firefox (obscures the focus indicator on links)
Line 1840 WCAG 2.2 AA F78 Section 508 (2017) AA F78
Attribute href not allowed on element.

1877<span class="sr-only" id="0lxw7">

1878</span>

1879</button>

The aria-labelledby attribute references a blank element.
Make sure aria-labelledby references an element containing text.
Line 1880 WCAG 2.2 A 4.1.2 Section 508 (2017) A 4.1.2
This button element is empty and has no accessible name.

A programmatically determined name allows screen readers to tell users what the control does. To add a name do one of the following:

  • Add text between the button start and end tags
  • Add a title attribute
  • Add an aria-label attribute
  • Add an aria-labelledby attribute
  • Add an img alt attribute if the button contains an img element
img elements with role=presentation or role=none are not included in the button's accessible name.
Line 1880 WCAG 2.2 A 4.1.2 Section 508 (2017) A 4.1.2
The CSS outline or border style on this element makes it difficult or impossible to see the link focus outline.
:focus and :not(:focus) have same outline:
Do not remove the default outline style, and change any border styles to avoid obscuring the focus outline around focusable elements. See :focus-visible for more information.

Using a border or outline style that obscures the focus ring causes problems for keyboard-only users in:

  • Chrome (obscures the focus indicator on links, buttons, dropdowns and range controls)
  • Firefox (obscures the focus indicator on links)
Line 1880 WCAG 2.2 AA F78 Section 508 (2017) AA F78
Attribute href not allowed on element.

1926<div class="Default_mediaWrapper__rO7Nk">

The aria-labelledby attribute references a blank element.
Make sure aria-labelledby references an element containing text.
Line 1927 WCAG 2.2 A 4.1.2 Section 508 (2017) A 4.1.2
This button element is empty and has no accessible name.

A programmatically determined name allows screen readers to tell users what the control does. To add a name do one of the following:

  • Add text between the button start and end tags
  • Add a title attribute
  • Add an aria-label attribute
  • Add an aria-labelledby attribute
  • Add an img alt attribute if the button contains an img element
img elements with role=presentation or role=none are not included in the button's accessible name.
Line 1927 WCAG 2.2 A 4.1.2 Section 508 (2017) A 4.1.2
The CSS outline or border style on this element makes it difficult or impossible to see the link focus outline.
:focus and :not(:focus) have same outline:
Do not remove the default outline style, and change any border styles to avoid obscuring the focus outline around focusable elements. See :focus-visible for more information.

Using a border or outline style that obscures the focus ring causes problems for keyboard-only users in:

  • Chrome (obscures the focus indicator on links, buttons, dropdowns and range controls)
  • Firefox (obscures the focus indicator on links)
Line 1927 WCAG 2.2 AA F78 Section 508 (2017) AA F78
Attribute href not allowed on element.
Line 1927 HTML5

1927<button type="button" href="" class="" aria-labelledby="e9xe3">

button elements containing only an img must have an alt attribute on the img.
Add an alt attribute describing the button action, or use alt="" with an aria-label on the button element.
Line 1928 WCAG 2.2 A F65 Section 508 (2017) A F65

Line 1997 HTML5 ARIA 1.2

1997<div class="FooterPartners_partner__tkir8" aria-label=" ">

img elements must have an accessible name.
Add an alt attribute describing the image, which screen readers voice instead of the image. Spacer images and purely decorative images should use alt="" without any global ARIA attributes. Do not use alt text containing only spaces since that's voiced as an unlabeled image.

Impact on users:

  • NVDA 2023.3 Chrome 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • NVDA 2023.3 FF 115 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • NVDA 2023.3 Edge 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 Chrome 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 FF 115 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 Edge 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • VoiceOver macOS 13.6 Safari 16.6 macOS 13.6.0 Reading: Image filename read out.
  • VoiceOver iOS 16.6 Safari iOS 16.6 iOS 16.6.1 Touch: Image filename read out, along with OCR text from image.
Line 1998 WCAG 2.2 A F65 Section 508 (2017) A F65
